gm mogrify -format 8BIM -bordercolor "#efefef01" -page 2380x3368 -gravity Center -density 50x50 -crop 20x20+5+5 -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -scale 20x20+5+5 -roll 50+30 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -rotate -90 -shave 1x1 -raise 50x30 -swirl 10 -charcoal 10 -border 50x50 -median 50 -paint 10 -edge 50 -quality 4 -implode 8 -colorspace CMYK -define cineon:colorspace=rgb -compose Plus  @@
gm mogrify -format 8BIM -fill "#1f1f1f" -mattecolor "#efefef01" -background "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -density 50x50 -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -roll 50+30 -thumbnail 38x25 -rotate "-90<" -sharpen 20x1 -blur 50 -swirl 10 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -compress LZMA -quality 0 -define dpx:colorspace=cineonlog  @@

gm convert -background "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -page 11x17 -gravity NorthWest -density 50x50 -crop 20x20+5+5 -repage 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -extent 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -motion-blur 50x1 -roll 50+30 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -raise 50x30 -90 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -quality 2 -colorspace GRAY -define dpx:colorspace=cineonlog  @@
gm convert -mattecolor "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -background "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -crop 20x20+5+5 -repage 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -extent 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resize 50x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -lat 20x20+5 -segment 0.015x1.5 -sharpen 20x1 -shave 1x1 -raise 50x30 -blur 50 -swirl 10 -charcoal 10 -paint 10 -emboss 50 -quality 0 -colorspace RGB -define dpx:swap-samples=true -compose In  @@
gm convert -format ART -fill "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -mattecolor "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -page 11x17 -gravity SouthEast -shadow 20x1 -size 384x256+64 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -chop 20x20+5+5 -scale 20x20+5+5 -resize 50x30 -lat 20x20+5 -segment 0.015x1.5 -shave 1x1 -shade 2x1 -swirl 10 -charcoal 10 -wave 30x30 -paint 10 -edge 50  @@

gm montage -format 8BIM -bordercolor "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -page 11x17 -gravity SouthEast -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resize 50x30 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -roll 50+30 -sharpen 20x1 -shade 2x1 -raise 50x30 -gaussian 30 -swirl 10 -border 50x50 -compress WebP -edge 50 -implode 8 -define pdf:stop-on-error=true -compose Divide  @@
gm mogrify -format 3FR -fill blue -mattecolor "#efefef01" -highlight-color "#efefef01" -shadow 20x1 -density 50x50 -size 384x256+64 -extent 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -sample 20x20+5+5 -roll 50+30 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -rotate "-90<" -shave 1x1 -shade 2x1 -gaussian 30 -90 -swirl 10 -charcoal 10 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -compress WebP -edge 50 -implode 8  @@
gm convert -format ART -fill "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -mattecolor "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -bordercolor blue -shadow 20x1 -density 50x50 -repage 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -rotate -90 -raise 50x30 -90 -charcoal 10 -border 50x50 -median 50 -paint 10 -compress WebP -emboss 50 -quality 2  @@
gm convert -format ART -mattecolor "#1f1f1f" -bordercolor blue -shadow 20x1 -density 50x50 -crop 20x20+5+5 -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -extent 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -roll 50+30 -rotate 180 -shave 1x1 -90 -swirl 10 -charcoal 10 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -emboss 50 -edge 50 -quality 0 -implode 8 -define dpx:colorspace=cineonlog -compose In  @@

gm montage -background blue -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -extent 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -roll 50+30 -thumbnail 38x25 -shave 1x1 -swirl 10 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -paint 10 -compress JPEG -emboss 50 -implode 8 -define tiff:strip-per-page=true -compose Atop  @@

gm mogrify -format BMP -list Color -bordercolor blue -size 384x256+64 -region 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -extent 20x20+5+5 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -sharpen 20x1 -raise 50x30 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -edge 50 -quality 1 -implode 8 -compose Atop  @@
gm convert -format 8BIM -list Color -fill "#efefef01" -highlight-color blue -bordercolor blue -crop 20x20+5+5 -size 384x256+64 -region 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -extent 20x20+5+5 -resize 50x30 -rotate "90>" -shave 1x1 -raise 50x30 -blur 50 -paint 10 -quality 1 -implode 8 -define jpeg:block-smoothing=true -compose Over  @@
gm convert -format 3FR -list Color -mattecolor "#efefef01" -bordercolor blue -page 11x17 -gravity SouthEast -shadow 20x1 -density 50x50 -crop 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -roll 50+30 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -shave 1x1 -shade 2x1 -blur 50 -gaussian 30 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -emboss 50 -edge 50 -define pdf:use-cropbox=true -compose In  @@
gm convert -format 3FR -bordercolor "#efefef01" -page 612x792 -gravity Center -shadow 20x1 -crop 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -gaussian 30 -90 -swirl 10 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -paint 10 -quality 2 -colorspace GRAY -define cineon:colorspace=rgb -compose Atop  @@

gm mogrify -format ART -list Module -fill "#efefef01" -mattecolor "#1f1f1f" -background "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -page 2380x3368 -gravity East -repage 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -chop 20x20+5+5 -extent 20x20+5+5 -resize 50x30 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -shave 1x1 -shade 2x1 -raise 50x30 -charcoal 10 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -paint 10 -emboss 50 -edge 50 -quality 3 -implode 8  @@
gm montage -format ART -list Resource -fill "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -mattecolor blue -highlight-color "#efefef01" -gravity SouthEast -shadow 20x1 -density 50x50 -repage 20x20+5+5 -scale 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -lat 20x20+5 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -rotate -90 -shade 2x1 -gaussian 30 -90 -swirl 10 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -paint 10 -emboss 50 -quality 3 -define jp2:rate=0.75 -compose Over  @@
gm montage -format ART -list Magic -highlight-color "#efefef01" -background "#efefef01" -density 50x50 -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -chop 20x20+5+5 -scale 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -lat 20x20+5 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -shave 1x1 -blur 50 -gaussian 30 -charcoal 10 -border 50x50 -emboss 50 -edge 50 -implode 8 -define jpeg:block-smoothing=true -compose In  @@
gm montage -mattecolor "#1f1f1f" -highlight-color "#1f1f1f" -bordercolor "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -gravity East -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -chop 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -scale 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -segment 0.015x1.5 -rotate "90>" -sharpen 20x1 -shave 1x1 -charcoal 10 -wave 30x30 -paint 10 -compress LZMA -emboss 50 -quality 0 -implode 8 -define tiff:report-warnings=true -compose Minus  @@
gm montage -format 3FR -list Delegate -highlight-color "#efefef01" -shadow 20x1 -density 50x50 -crop 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -extent 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resize 50x30 -resample 30x30 -lat 20x20+5 -roll 50+30 -sharpen 20x1 -shade 2x1 -gaussian 30 -border 50x50 -edge 50 -quality 4 -implode 8 -define dpx:swap-samples=true -compose Over  @@

gm convert -bordercolor "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -shadow 20x1 -density 50x50 -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -chop 20x20+5+5 -extent 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resize 50x30 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -lat 20x20+5 -roll 50+30 -segment 0.015x1.5 -sharpen 20x1 -shave 1x1 -90 -charcoal 10 -border 50x50 -median 50 -compress BZip -edge 50 -quality 3 -define dpx:pixel-endian=msb  @@

gm montage -list Delegate -mattecolor "#1f1f1f" -highlight-color blue -page +100+200 -gravity East -shadow 20x1 -repage 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -extent 20x20+5+5 -scale 20x20+5+5 -thumbnail 38x25 -segment 0.015x1.5 -shave 1x1 -raise 50x30 -blur 50 -gaussian 30 -swirl 10 -charcoal 10 -wave 30x30 -paint 10 -emboss 50 -edge 50 -quality 2 -implode 8 -define jpeg:block-smoothing=true  @@
gm montage -list Resource -highlight-color "rgb(65000,65000,65535)" -gravity SouthEast -shadow 20x1 -crop 20x20+5+5 -size 384x256+64 -repage 20x20+5+5 -region 20x20+5+5 -unsharp 0x1.0+1.0+0.05 -extent 20x20+5+5 -geometry 20x20+5+5 -resample 30x30 -sample 20x20+5+5 -motion-blur 50x1 -roll 50+30 -sharpen 20x1 -90 -border 50x50 -wave 30x30 -median 50 -edge 50 -define tiff:alpha=associated -compose Plus  @@
